# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="1046a-102">Veraltete Typen in .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1046a-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="1046a-103">In den Tabellen dieses Artikels sind die Typen aufgeführt, die in [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] und [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)] veraltet sind, geordnet nach Assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1046a-103">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1046a-104">Über die nachfolgenden Links finden Sie eine Liste der veralteten Typen und empfohlenen Alternativen in den jeweiligen Assemblys.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1046a-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1046a-105">Da diese Typen veraltet sind, sind alle ihrer Member ebenfalls veraltet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1046a-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1046a-106">Eine Liste weiterer veralteter Member in der .NET Framework-Klassenbibliothek finden Sie unter [Veraltete Member](obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1046a-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

<a name="obsolete_types_in_system_assemblies"></a>
